This book will help you understand and use idioms better. It contains over 300 of today's most common idioms. \r\n\r\nIdioms add color to the language. Master idioms and your speech will be less awkward, less foreign. You'll also understand more of what you read and hear. Often a student of English tries to translate idioms word-for-word, or literally.
